167.2(1): bar mdzod/ smon lam chen po'i thugs dang 'dir gshegs la/ bdag dang mtha' 
167.3(1): yas sems can thams cad dang / yon bdag rgyu sbyor 'khor dang bcas pa rnams/
167.4(1): bla med 'bras bu rtag tu thob par shog /ces stobs chen 'phrin las kyi sgo nas 
167.5(1): bstod pa'o/ /
167.6(1): da ni kun dbyings sku lnga'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs rnams la/ bkra shis yon 
167.7(1): tan gyi sgo nas bstod de/ phyag rgya gser gyi nya mo ltar bca' la/ sngags brjod pa/
167.8(1): oM na ma b+hud+d+ha sa mun ta/ A dar ba dar du na ma na re/ de rgya tsan+d+ra she tsu tra ya dza ye 
167.9(1): swahA/ zhes pas bde bar gshegs pa'i thugs las 'od zer 'phros pas/ 'jig 
167.10(1): rten gyi khams thams cad/ legs par bya ba'i don dang yon tan dpag tu med 
167.11(1): pas khyab par bsam la/ tshigs su bcad de gsungs pa/ kun khyab nam mkha'i 
167.12(1): gzi mdangs can/ kun dbyings gtso bo 'khor bcas dang / mkha' la rang bzhin 
167.13(1): rdzogs pa yi/ longs spyod rdzogs sku 'khor bcas dang / ma bcos mnyam par gnas 
167.14(1): pa yi/ ngo bo nyid sku 'khor bcas dang / klong las thugs rje 'byung ba yi/ cir yang 
167.15(1): sprul sku 'khor bcas dang / bdag gzhan don gnyis mthar phyin pa'i/ mngon par 
167.16(1): byang chub 'khor bcas dang / 'khor ba nyon mongs gzhom pa yi/ sku gsum me lha 
167.17(1): 'khor bcas dang / thabs chen mkha' la rol pa yi/ mkha' 'gying dkar po 'khor 
167.18(1): bcas dang / mthu chen dbang dang ldan pa yi/ snang ba 'od ldan 'khor bcas dang /

167.20(1): bo lha dgu la/ bkra shis gzhal yas bde chen 'dir/ bla med mchod pa'i rgyan 
167.21(1): bshams pa/ bdud rtsi chu bo'i rgyun bzhin du/ mchod pa'i rgyun kyang mi chad cing /

168.2(1): 'gyur med g.yung drung sku 'chang ba'i/ gsal ba rang 'byung 'khor bcas dang /

168.4(1): gsung dang ldan pa yi/ bye brag dngos med 'khor bcas dang / ma btsal lhun gyis 
168.5(1): grub pa yi/ dga' ba don grub 'khor bcas dang / nyon mongs nad rnams sel ba 
168.6(1): yi/ bdud rtsi rgyal ba 'khor bcas dang / thabs cad yongs la snyoms pa yi/ zhi

168.8(1): phud rgyal ba 'khor bcas dang / ngan song gdar thag gcod pa yi/ byams pa

168.13(1): gsas btsan po 'khor bcas dang / mnyam nyid ye shes ngang ldan pa'i/ rgod
